Introduction

This documentation aims to provide all the information you need to work with our API.

As you scroll, you'll see code examples for working with the API in different programming languages in the dark area to the right (or as part of the content on mobile). You can switch the language used with the tabs at the top right (or from the nav menu at the top left on mobile).

Base URL

http://localhost

Authenticating requests

This API is not authenticated.

Endpoints

Display all categories

This method is used to display all categories.

Example request:
curl --request GET \
    --get "http://localhost/api/categories" \
    --header "Content-Type: application/json" \
    --header "Accept: application/json"
const url = new URL(
    "http://localhost/api/categories"
);

const headers = {
    "Content-Type": "application/json",
    "Accept": "application/json",
};

fetch(url, {
    method: "GET",
    headers,
}).then(response => response.json());

Example response (200):

Show headers 
cache-control: no-cache, private
content-type: application/json
x-ratelimit-limit: 60
x-ratelimit-remaining: 59
access-control-allow-origin: *
 

{
    "data": []
}
Received response:
Request failed with error:

Request      

GET api/categories

Display a listing of the resource.

This method is used to display all projects.

Example request:
curl --request GET \
    --get "http://localhost/api/projects" \
    --header "Content-Type: application/json" \
    --header "Accept: application/json"
const url = new URL(
    "http://localhost/api/projects"
);

const headers = {
    "Content-Type": "application/json",
    "Accept": "application/json",
};

fetch(url, {
    method: "GET",
    headers,
}).then(response => response.json());

Request      

GET api/projects

Store a newly created category in storage.

This method is used to create a new category.

Example request:
curl --request POST \
    "http://localhost/api/categories" \
    --header "Content-Type: application/json" \
    --header "Accept: application/json" \
    --data "{
    \"name\": \"ptvocjpvpguprhomydsimtljptdwfrgfd\"
}"

const url = new URL(
    "http://localhost/api/categories"
);

const headers = {
    "Content-Type": "application/json",
    "Accept": "application/json",
};

let body = {
    "name": "ptvocjpvpguprhomydsimtljptdwfrgfd"
};

fetch(url, {
    method: "POST",
    headers,
    body: JSON.stringify(body),
}).then(response => response.json());
Received response:
Request failed with error:

Request      

POST api/categories

Body Parameters

name  string  

Must be at least 3 characters. Must not be greater than 200 characters.

DIsplay single category

This method is used to display a single category.

Example request:
curl --request GET \
    --get "http://localhost/api/categories/20" \
    --header "Content-Type: application/json" \
    --header "Accept: application/json"
const url = new URL(
    "http://localhost/api/categories/20"
);

const headers = {
    "Content-Type": "application/json",
    "Accept": "application/json",
};

fetch(url, {
    method: "GET",
    headers,
}).then(response => response.json());

Example response (404):

x-ratelimit-remaining: 58
access-control-allow-origin: *
